< review>
I have been their customer for almost 10 years until I last brought my car in for the free service that was included with the purchase of new tires. The tires needed balancing and pressure check. I specifically asked the mechanic to let me know if he sees anything that needs to be fixed. When he was done, he said that he corrected the tire pressure and did not see any other problem.
As soon as I left the shop the car was continuously pulling to the right. I returned the next day and I asked the manager to have the car inspected again, because the car did not behave like  that before the service. A young mechanic immediately noticed, without even taking the wheel out, that the front right tire had a separation and it formed a bubble.
Further looking into the records of the previous day work, we found out that the mechanic reported the previous day that the car has 20k more miles than it actually had, to force us out of warranty and into buying new tires when we discover the problem. What a despicable individual...(and possibly a company policy?) They blamed the tire damage on the road conditions.
I have asked for a second opinion about what could have caused the sudden tire separation during the service and I was told that the most likely cause was a brief hyperinflation of the tire, which I have suspected all along. Would you return to a shop that put your family in danger through such despicable acts? NEVER!<//review>

< review>
Best ice cream in town! Handel's has so many delicious flavors, my only complaint would be that it's so hard to choose my favorite! They make new ice cream every day, keeping things fresh. The atmosphere is clean and organized, making ordering very efficient. They have nice outdoor seating, but there are tables inside as well. The service is unbeatable, and they're a great employer for teens looking for a first job. Lauren was especially great; she was able to memorize our order for 6 people in one try. Handel's has been a great edition to Folsom, and my family looks forward to visiting a lot this summer!< /review>

< text>
The 1st time I came here, I ordered the 4 scoop sampler to try different flavors and they were all amazing. They did not skimp on ingredients, there were so many whole pistachios in pistachio, whole cherries in black cherry, bug chunks of peanut butter and brownie and so much flavor in the monkey. <rate>5< /rate>< Review>
Social Networking plays an important role within our global society. It allows individuals to connect with each other, keep in touch with old friends, and gives society the ability to explore your interests and hobbies. The famous social networking site, Facebook, has swept the social media scene since its establishment in 2004. Recently, Facebook has accumulated billions of dollars in the global market. Shandi Raice reports that Facebook‚Äôs worth will rise to 140 billion dollars by 2015.  Mark Zuckerberg, the creater of Facebook, was named Time magazines man of the year in 2010. Zuckerberg created this social network in the dorm room of Harvard University and the network spread like wildfire.
These issues include privacy concerns and censorship, psychological distress, and inappropriate content. First, I will go into the privacy concerns associated with Facebook. This social networking website allows the user to customize information on their profiles allowing the website to send them information that may appeal to them. Facebook only sends information that they think the user will enjoy. Facebook interprets the user‚Äôs particular interests and presents it to them in an easy to read website page called a ‚Äúnews feed.‚Äù This news feed only present information that Facebook‚Äôs believes the user will enjoy but censors information that would not be appealing to the user‚Äôs particular interests. For example, I was accessing Facebook reading articles that were posted from many on my conservative friends. I have one liberal friend that presents articles with interesting points of view on many of our current politicians.< /Review>
